SQL> -- MRE_Time_DIM_L0
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Time_DIM_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT DISTINCT
  3          TO_CHAR(d.dates, 'YYYYMMDY') AS Time_ID,
  4          TO_CHAR(d.dates, 'YYYY') AS Year,
  5          TO_NUMBER(TO_CHAR(d.dates, 'MM'), '99') AS Month,
  6          TO_CHAR(d.dates, 'DY') AS Day_of_Week
  7      FROM (
  8          SELECT DISTINCT Sale_Date AS DATES FROM MRE_Sale
  9              WHERE Sale_Date IS NOT NULL
 10          UNION 
 11          SELECT DISTINCT Rent_Start_Date FROM MRE_Rent
 12              WHERE Rent_Start_Date IS NOT NULL
 13          UNION 
 14          SELECT DISTINCT Rent_End_Date FROM MRE_Rent
 15              WHERE Rent_End_Date IS NOT NULL
 16          ) d        
 17  );

Table MRE_TIME_DIM_L0 created.

SQL> 
SQL> ALTER TABLE MRE_Time_DIM_L0
  2  ADD Season_ID NUMBER;

Table MRE_TIME_DIM_L0 altered.

SQL> 
SQL> UPDATE MRE_Time_DIM_L0
  2  SET Season_ID = 
  3      (CASE
  4          WHEN Month = 12 OR Month BETWEEN 1 AND 2 THEN 1
  5          WHEN Month BETWEEN 3 AND 5 THEN 2
  6          WHEN Month BETWEEN 6 AND 8 THEN 3
  7          WHEN Month BETWEEN 9 AND 11 THEN 4
  8      END);

68 rows updated.

SQL> ---------------------------
SQL> -- Implement fact tables --
SQL> ---------------------------
SQL> -- MRE_Sale_FACT_L0
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Sale_FACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT 
  3          s.Agent_Person_ID,
  4          s.Client_Person_ID,
  5          TO_CHAR(s.Sale_Date, 'YYYYMMDY') AS Time_ID,
  6          s.Property_ID,
  7          s.Price AS Total_Sales_Price,
  8          COUNT(s.Sale_ID) AS Number_of_Sales
  9      FROM MRE_Sale s, MRE_Property p
 10      WHERE s.Property_ID = p.Property_ID
 11      AND s.Client_Person_ID IS NOT NULL
 12      AND s.Sale_Date IS NOT NULL
 13      GROUP BY s.Agent_Person_ID, s.Client_Person_ID, TO_CHAR(s.Sale_Date, 'YYYYMMDY'), s.Property_ID, s.Price
 14  );

Table MRE_SALE_FACT_L0 created.

SQL> 
SQL> -- MRE_Rent_FACT_L0
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Rent_TempFACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT
  3          r.Agent_Person_ID,
  4          r.Client_Person_ID,
  5          r.Property_ID,
  6          r.Rent_Start_Date,
  7          r.Rent_End_Date,        
  8          p.Property_No_of_Bedrooms AS Number_of_bedrooms,
  9          COUNT(pf.Feature_Code) AS Number_of_features,
 10          ROUND((r.Price / 7) * (Rent_End_Date - Rent_Start_Date), 2) AS Total_Rent_Fee,
 11          COUNT(DISTINCT r.Rent_ID) AS Number_of_Rent
 12      FROM MRE_Rent r, MRE_Property p, MRE_Property_Feature pf
 13      WHERE r.Property_ID = p.Property_ID
 14      AND pf.Property_ID = p.Property_ID
 15      AND r.Client_Person_ID IS NOT NULL
 16      AND r.Rent_Start_Date IS NOT NULL
 17      AND r.Rent_End_Date IS NOT NULL
 18      GROUP BY r.Agent_Person_ID, r.Client_Person_ID, r.Property_ID, r.Rent_Start_Date, r.Rent_End_Date, 
 19               p.Property_No_of_Bedrooms, ROUND((r.Price / 7) * (Rent_End_Date - Rent_Start_Date), 2)
 20  );

Table MRE_RENT_TEMPFACT_L0 created.

SQL> 
SQL> ALTER TABLE MRE_Rent_TempFACT_L0
  2  ADD (Rental_Period_ID NUMBER,
  3       Scale_ID NUMBER,
  4       Feature_Cat_ID NUMBER);

Table MRE_RENT_TEMPFACT_L0 altered.

SQL> 
SQL> UPDATE MRE_Rent_TempFACT_L0
  2  SET Rental_Period_ID = 
  3          (CASE
  4              WHEN MONTHS_BETWEEN(Rent_Start_Date, Rent_End_Date) < 6 THEN 1
  5              WHEN MONTHS_BETWEEN(Rent_Start_Date, Rent_End_Date) BETWEEN 6 AND 12 THEN 2
  6              WHEN MONTHS_BETWEEN(Rent_Start_Date, Rent_End_Date) > 12 THEN 3
  7          END),    
  8      Scale_ID = 
  9          (CASE
 10              WHEN Number_of_bedrooms <= 1 THEN 1
 11              WHEN Number_of_bedrooms BETWEEN 2 AND 3 THEN 2
 12              WHEN Number_of_bedrooms BETWEEN 4 AND 6 THEN 3            
 13              WHEN Number_of_bedrooms BETWEEN 7 AND 10 THEN 4            
 14              WHEN Number_of_bedrooms > 10 THEN 5
 15          END),
 16      Feature_Cat_ID = 
 17          (CASE
 18              WHEN Number_of_features < 10 THEN 1
 19              WHEN Number_of_features BETWEEN 10 AND 20 THEN 2
 20              WHEN Number_of_features > 20 THEN 3
 21          END)
 22  ;

1,116 rows updated.

SQL> 
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Rent_FACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT
  3          Agent_Person_ID,
  4          Client_Person_ID,
  5          Property_ID,
  6          to_char(Rent_Start_Date, 'YYYYMMDY') as rent_start_date,
  7          to_char(Rent_End_Date, 'YYYYMMDY') as rent_end_date,
  8          Rental_Period_ID,
  9          Scale_ID,
 10          Feature_Cat_ID,
 11          Total_Rent_Fee,
 12          Number_of_Rent
 13      FROM MRE_Rent_TempFACT_L0 
 14  );

Table MRE_RENT_FACT_L0 created.

SQL> 
SQL> -- MRE_Client_FACT_L0
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Client_TempFACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT 
  3          Person_ID AS Client_Person_ID,
  4          Max_Budget,
  5          COUNT(Person_ID) AS Number_of_Clients
  6      FROM MRE_Client
  7      GROUP BY Person_ID, Min_Budget, Max_Budget
  8  );

Table MRE_CLIENT_TEMPFACT_L0 created.

  2  ADD Budget_ID VARCHAR2(2);

Table MRE_CLIENT_TEMPFACT_L0 altered.

  2  SET Budget_ID = 
  3      (CASE
  4          WHEN Max_Budget >= 0 AND Max_Budget <= 1000 THEN 1
  5          WHEN Max_Budget >= 1001 AND Max_Budget <= 100000 THEN 3
  6          WHEN Max_Budget >= 100001 AND Max_Budget <= 10000000 THEN 5
  7      END);

3,334 rows updated.

SQL> 
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Client_FACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT 
  3          Client_Person_ID,
  4          Budget_ID,
  5          Number_of_Clients
  6      FROM MRE_Client_TempFACT_L0
  7  );

Table MRE_CLIENT_FACT_L0 created.

SQL> 
SQL> -- MRE_Agent_FACT_L0
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Agent_FACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT * FROM 
  3      (SELECT a.person_id as agent_person_id, SUM(nvl(s.price, 0)) + nvl(SUM(nvl(r.price, 0)/7*(r.rent_end_date - r.rent_start_date)), 0) as total_earnings
  4      FROM mre_agent a, mre_sale s, mre_rent r
  5          WHERE a.person_id = s.agent_person_id (+)
  6          AND a.person_id = r.agent_person_id (+)
  7              GROUP BY a.person_id)
  8  );

Table MRE_AGENT_FACT_L0 created.

SQL> 
SQL> -- MRE_Visit_FACT_L0
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Visit_FACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT DISTINCT 
  3          Client_Person_ID,
  4          Agent_Person_ID,
  5          Property_ID,
  6          TO_CHAR(Visit_Date, 'YYYYMMDY') AS Time_ID,
  7          COUNT(*) AS Number_of_Visits
  8      FROM MRE_Visit 
  9      GROUP BY Client_Person_ID, Agent_Person_ID, Property_ID, TO_CHAR(Visit_Date, 'YYYYMMDY')
 10  );

Table MRE_VISIT_FACT_L0 created.

SQL> 
SQL> -- MRE_Advert_FACT_L0
SQL> CREATE TABLE MRE_Advert_FACT_L0 AS (
  2      SELECT DISTINCT
  3          pa.Property_ID,
  4          pa.Advert_ID,
  5          TO_CHAR(p.Property_Date_Added, 'YYYYMMDY') AS Time_ID,
  6          COUNT(pa.Advert_ID) AS Number_of_Adverts
  7      FROM MRE_Property_Advert pa, MRE_Property p 
  8      WHERE pa.Property_ID = p.Property_ID
  9      GROUP BY pa.Property_ID, pa.Advert_ID, TO_CHAR(p.Property_Date_Added, 'YYYYMMDY')
 10  );

Table MRE_ADVERT_FACT_L0 created.
